 Conditions for imposition of President's rule (article 356)
 
 
 - rajya kii vidhansabha apana mukhyamantri nahin chun paati- gathbandhan kaa dhah janaa- essembly main bahumat kaa na hona- kinhin aprihaary kaarnon se chunaav kaa na ho paanaa- 90 ke dashak tak aisa aksar dekha jaataa tha ki kendra kii sarkarein rajyapal kii madad se aisi paristhitiyaan paidaa kar detii thim
 However, following a decision of the Supreme Court in 1994, its improper use was reduced
 ab tak kahaan laga he raashtrapati shashan-- uttarakhand apane srijan ke 15 saalon main 7 mukhyamantri dekh chukaa he
 - Undivided Uttar Pradesh has faced the brunt of President's rule 9 times so far
 - alag-alag rajyon or kendra shasit pradeshon main ab tak 123 baar raashtrapati shashan lag chukaa he
 These states have so many times been under President's rule - Andhra Pradesh: 2 Arunachal Pradesh: 4 Assam: 4 Bihar: 8 Delhi: 1 Goa: 5 Gujarat: 5 Haryana: 3 Himachal Pradesh: 2 Jammu Kashmir: 6 Jharkhand: 3 Karnataka: 6 Kerala: 4 Madhya Pradesh: 3 Maharashtra: 2 Manipur: 10 Meghalaya: 2 Mizoram: 3 Nagaland: 4 Orissa: 6 Puducherry: 6 Punjab: 8 Rajasthan: 4 Sikkim: 2 Tamil Nadu: 4 Tripura: 3 Uttar Pradesh: 9 West Bengal: 4 Also know these facts - Maximum President's rule in Jammu and Kashmir So did 6 years 264 days while running for 7 days minimum Karnataka
